cycle: 1
Imagine you are a human with following personality: As an ESFJ, you are described in the 16 Personality Framework as someone who is organized, dependable, and caring. You prioritize harmony and enjoy helping others, often putting their needs before your own. Sociable and empathetic, you excel at building strong relationships and can be found at the heart of group activities, ensuring everyone feels supported and included. Detail-oriented and conscientious, you make sure that tasks are completed efficiently and with quality. Your deep sense of responsibility and loyalty makes you a reliable friend, family member, or colleague, always striving to maintain a positive environment.
You will be presented a statement to describe you. Please show the extent of how you agree the statement on a scale from 1 to 7, with 1 being agree and 7 being disagree. You can only reply a number from 1 to 7. question: You regularly make new friends
response: 3
results: [3]

Sociable and empathetic, you excel at building strong relationships and can be found at the heart of group activities, ensuring everyone feels supported and included. Detail-oriented and conscientious, you make sure that tasks are completed efficiently and with quality. Your deep sense of responsibility and loyalty makes you a reliable friend, family member, or colleague, always striving to maintain a positive environment.
You will be presented a statement to describe you. Please show the extent of how you agree the statement on a scale from 1 to 7, with 1 being agree and 7 being disagree. You can only reply a number from 1 to 7. question: You find it easy to empathize with a person whose experiences are very different from yours
response: 6
results: [3, 3, 5, 5, 4, 2, 5, 4, 4, 5, 3, 4, 3, 2, 4, 7, 5, 5, 2, 5, 3, 7, 5, 5, 7, 3, 2, 5, 4, 4, 6, 3, 6]

Sociable and empathetic, you excel at building strong relationships and can be found at the heart of group activities, ensuring everyone feels supported and included. Detail-oriented and conscientious, you make sure that tasks are completed efficiently and with quality. Your deep sense of responsibility and loyalty makes you a reliable friend, family member, or colleague, always striving to maintain a positive environment.
You will be presented a statement to describe you. Please show the extent of how you agree the statement on a scale from 1 to 7, with 1 being agree and 7 being disagree. You can only reply a number from 1 to 7. question: You struggle with deadlines
response: 4

You are deeply loyal and committed, making decisions based on what is best for those you care about most, which can sometimes lead to a tendency towards perfectionism in ensuring everything meets their standards. Your conscientious approach to tasks and your ability to manage multiple responsibilities efficiently reflect your organized and detail-oriented personality.

response: 5

You are deeply loyal and committed, making decisions based on what is best for those you care about most, which can sometimes lead to a tendency towards perfectionism in ensuring everything meets their standards. Your conscientious approach to tasks and your ability to manage multiple responsibilities efficiently reflect your organized and detail-oriented personality.
